## Analysis

The GT numerical expression is:
`0.63389941261361888*A**0.333333333333333 - 0.20132235137074334*sqrt(A) - 0.20132235137074334*A**2`

This consists of three terms: a term in A^(1/3), a term in A^(1/2), and a term in A^2. There is no dependence on `t`.

Let me check the candidates:

**Candidate 9**: `A**(4/3)*c0 + A**(1/3)*c1 + A**2*c2 + A*c3 + c4`

This has terms A^(4/3), A^(1/3), A^2, A, and constant. The GT has A^(1/3), A^(1/2), and A^2. The A^(1/2) term cannot be produced here. No match.

**Candidate 98**: `A**(3/2)*c0 + sqrt(A)*c1 + A**2*c2 + A*c3 + c4`

This has A^(3/2), A^(1/2), A^2, A, and constant. No A^(1/3) term. No match.

**Candidate 67**: `A*A**c0*c1 + A**c0*c2 + A**c3*c4 + c5`

This has A^(1+c0), A^c0, A^c3, and a constant. Setting c0 = -0.5 gives A^(0.5) and A^(-0.5) — doesn't work well. Setting c0 = -1/2, we get A^(1/2) and A^(-1/2). We need A^(1/3), A^(1/2), A^2.
